[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m939[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/reformat.[0m[1;92mc:1711[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1713[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1711[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mconvertResult == AVIF_RESULT_NOT_IMPLEMENTED[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1712[0m[39m:            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m If we get here, there is no fast path for this combination. [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTime to be slow![0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1713[0m[39m:            convertResult = [0m[1;35mavifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mimage, rgb, state, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malphaMultiplyMode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of the Issue[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and evaluation report, I have identified the root[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause of the dynamic-stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability occurs in the spill upsampling algorithm at **line [0m[1;36m812[0m[39m** in [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/reformat.c` within the `avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow` function. The issue [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvolves **missing or incomplete bounds checking** before accessing stack-allocated[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvariable-length arrays [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`uspill_image` and `vspill_image`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with adjacency offsets.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Two problematic code regions:**[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Lines [0m[1;36m774[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m782[0m[39m**: Incomplete bounds checking[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Only checks for overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`i + adjCol >= image->width`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Missing underflow check** when `[0m[33mi[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` and `[0m[33madjCol[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m`, resulting in negative [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marray index[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Same issue for `j` and `adjRow`[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Lines [0m[1;36m800[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m818[0m[39m**: Complete absence of bounds checking [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPRIMARY ISSUE[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Variables `a` and `b` are calculated identically to `adjCol` and `adjRow`[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **No bounds checking whatsoever** before array accesses at lines [0m[1;36m812[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m817[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m812[0m[39m is where ASan detected the [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte read overflow[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### The Correct Pattern[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase already contains the **correct bounds checking pattern** at lines [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m912[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m939[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbilinear upsampling[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mi == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mi == [0m[1;39m([0m[39mimage->width - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mi % [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    uAdjCol = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mj == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mj == [0m[1;39m([0m[39mimage->height - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mj % [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    uAdjRow = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis pattern explicitly checks:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Underflow**: `i == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` or `j == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mprevents negative indices[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Overflow**: Last position with odd parity [0m[1;39m([0m[39mprevents accessing beyond array [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounds[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Fix Incomplete Bounds Checking [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m774[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m782[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace the incomplete bounds checking with the correct pattern:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Current code:**[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint adjCol = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi%[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint adjRow = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj%[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m check the bounds[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi + adjCol >= image->width[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    adjCol = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj + adjRow >= image->height[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    adjRow = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fixed code:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint adjCol = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi%[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint adjRow = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj%[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m check the bounds for both underflow and overflow[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mi == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mi == [0m[1;39m([0m[39mimage->width - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mi % [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    adjCol = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mj == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mj == [0m[1;39m([0m[39mimage->height - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mj % [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    adjRow = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Add Missing Bounds Checking [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m800[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m818[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdd bounds checking for variables `a` and `b` before the array accesses:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Current code:**[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mimage->height * image->width[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m >= [0m[1;36m0x1000[0m[39m && total_spill > [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mimage->height * [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39melse[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        a = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj % [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39melse[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        b = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fixed code:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mimage->height * image->width[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m >= [0m[1;36m0x1000[0m[39m && total_spill > [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mimage->height * [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        b = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39melse[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        b = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Add bounds checking for a and b[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mi == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mi == [0m[1;39m([0m[39mimage->width - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mi % [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        a = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mj == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mj == [0m[1;39m([0m[39mimage->height - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mj % [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        b = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is the Optimal Approach[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Follows Existing Codebase Pattern**: The fix replicates the proven bounds [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecking logic already used at lines [0m[1;36m912[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m939[0m[39m for bilinear upsampling in the same [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Mathematically Sound**: Setting the adjustment to [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m when at boundaries means [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe spill remains on the current pixel, which is equivalent to having no adjacent [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpixel available - a scenario the algorithm already handles implicitly.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Minimal Code Changes**: Only adds/fixes bounds checking without altering the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcore spill distribution algorithm.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Preserves Functionality**: The spill upsampling algorithm's core logic remains[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Spill calculation and distribution pattern[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Dampening threshold logic  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Iterative convergence mechanism [0m[1;39m([0m[39mup to [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m iterations[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Early termination conditions[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Evaluation Report[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Fixes line [0m[1;36m812[0m[39m overflow**: The added bounds checking for `a` and `b` prevents [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte read beyond buffer bounds detected by ASan[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Handles underflow cases**: Explicitly checks `i == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` and `j == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` to prevent [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnegative array indices[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Handles overflow cases**: Checks edge conditions [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`i == width-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`, `j == [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheight-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` with odd parity[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Works for all image sizes**: Handles edge cases like 1x1, 2x2 images that [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing may generate[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect**: Boundary pixels may have slightly different spill distribution [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatterns.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation**: [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This is expected behavior - boundary pixels naturally have fewer neighbors[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The algorithm already accounts for this in corner and edge pixels[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The visual impact is negligible as boundary pixels are a small fraction of the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimage[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The reference implementation proves this approach produces correct output[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe bilinear upsampling code at lines [0m[1;36m912[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m939[0m[39m uses this exact pattern successfully,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdemonstrating it's the established and tested approach for handling adjacency [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffsets in this codebase.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe previous patch added lines [0m[1;36m809[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m815[0m[39m with incorrect bounds checking logic that [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis patch attempted to fix the issue but was placed AFTER the incorrect [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalculation, so it would override the value. The correct approach is to integrate [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe bounds checking INTO the calculation logic, not apply it afterward.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Is the Optimal Approach[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Proven Pattern**: This fix uses the exact same bounds checking logic already [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuccessfully employed in the bilinear upsampling code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m912[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m939[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, ensuring [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsistency and reliability.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Complete Coverage**: Both locations [0m[1;39m([0m[39madjCol/adjRow and a/b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are fixed with the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msame pattern, eliminating all buffer overflow vulnerabilities.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Correct Logic Flow**: The check-then-calculate pattern ensures offsets are [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnever set to invalid values, unlike the calculate-then-check approach which still [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrisks undefined behavior in the comparison.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Handles All Edge Cases**:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Underflow: `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mi == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mj == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` prevents negative indices[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Overflow: `[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mi == [0m[1;39m([0m[39mimage->width - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mi % [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` prevents indices >= [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwidth for odd positions[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Parity-based direction: Odd pixels look forward [0m[1;39m([0m[39m+[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, even pixels look [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbackward [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Same Algorithm**: The spill redistribution algorithm remains unchanged - we're[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monly fixing the bounds checking.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Same Access Pattern**: When not at edges, the offset values remain identical [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto the original code.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Edge Behavior**: At boundaries, setting offset to [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m means the pixel references[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mitself, which is the safest fallback and maintains the spill distribution [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvariant.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Functional Changes**: The fix only affects the calculation of offset [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalues, not the actual spill redistribution operations or convergence logic.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Evaluation Report Issues[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Initial crash at line [0m[1;36m812[0m[39m**: Fixed by adding proper bounds checking for [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvariables `a` and `b`.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Post-patch crash at line [0m[1;36m788[0m[39m**: Fixed by replacing the incomplete bounds [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecking for `adjCol` and `adjRow` with the complete check-then-calculate pattern.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Both locations addressed**: Unlike the previous patch which only partially [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maddressed one location, this fix comprehensively addresses both vulnerable code [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msections.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Performance**: The new logic has slightly more branching, but this is [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnegligible compared to the floating-point calculations in the spill algorithm, and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe crash-free operation far outweighs any minor performance impact.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Algorithm Behavior at Edges**: Setting offsets to [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m at boundaries means edge [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpixels don't redistribute spill to neighbors outside the image. This is correct [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior and prevents the overflow. The algorithm will still converge, just with [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39medge pixels potentially retaining more spill.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Consistency**: Using the same pattern as lines [0m[1;36m912[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m939[0m[39m ensures the spill [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mupsampling behaves consistently with bilinear upsampling at image boundaries.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Reference to Similar Solutions[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe reference implementation at lines [0m[1;36m912[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m939[0m[39m in the same file demonstrates this [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexact pattern has been successfully used for bilinear upsampling without issues. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis provides strong evidence that the proposed fix is correct and will work [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreliably.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
